4<//rate>
<Review>First time coming to a Lechon style place. As we came in the delicious smell of the roasted pork filed the air. The place is simply decorated with plastic chairs and metal and plastic tables. Walking up to the counter we saw all the offering they had on display. The best of all was the roasted pork laying there in it all it crunchy glory. Mmm yummy!!!
So being my first time I ordered one of each. Well except the blood, yup blood (pig's blood) not to fond of the irony taste of it. Ok, got all of the other items the pork stew, the chicken stew, and the veggies. It came with white steamed rice and noodles. The chicken Stew tasted like chicken adobo and very tasty. The pork stew had a good flavor. ( it looked as they used the leftover pork to make the stew). The best was yet to come. The roasted pork was crispy and the meat soft and tender. The crispy skin had a awesome flavor. Yummy!!! The pork had nice sweet flavor. Mmmm.
Overall this place is delicious if you're in the mood for roasted pork. I will definitely be back again. Enjoy everyone.</Review><Pics>None</Pics>< Response>
None</Response>

<Text>I went into the shop to get the service records on a car I bought. I was told all records were wiped clean in November 2017 by accident.  Next I went on carfax, guess what- Menifee Transmission never reports to car fax.  How do you not spend  $20 on a flash drive to keep a copy of your records safe? Find a shop with better business practices.< /Text><pics>None</pics><response>{'time': 1549069078331, 'text': "Unfortunately, our hard drive was wiped and we have since made changes to ensure it doesn't happen again, and it is not as simple and cheap as a $20 flash drive, our database is much more complicated then that.  However, I would like to mention that auto repair shops have never been required to report to Carfax.  From a quick look at Carfax's website it seems that auto repair facilities can pay a premium to Carfax and become an authorized shop, these shops more then likely, report the maintenance.  Reporting to Carfax is not required or mandatory, it is only an advertising option for auto repair facilities to get exposure and customers.  I would also like to add, when buying a used vehicle you should request copies of all service records from the seller and if they cannot provide them then you ask them to obtain such records prior to the purchase.  Used vehicles are normally buyer beware and sold as is. Also, even if our system had not been damaged, we would not have provided those records to you unless we had permission from the individual who owned the car previously, otherwise it is a violation of privacy. < Review>
Of the many vets I have worked with, Dr. Hazanow ranks at the very top. She helped us care for Aidan, our Irish Setter dog, in his elder years. He enjoyed a long life for his breed, but the last couple of years was tough, as he developed bladder disease and complications. Dr. Hazanow provided empathic problem-solving care that was clinically competent and highly attuned to both Aidan's needs and our needs as his caregivers. Never were we rushed through an appointment. Charges are reasonable and I never felt that anything being recommended--procedures, medications, or other care products--had any taint of profit motive. Indeed, Dr. Hazanow several times suggested cost-effective solutions available from the drugstore or the supermarket. When she was not available, Drs. Knobel and Whitaker could also be relied on to provide excellent patient and family centered care, and the support staff were competent and very helpful. A couple minor front desk problems I experienced could have happened anywhere and the staff were apologetic and quick to fix them. Seven Hills is a veterinary practice and facility where you and your family can expect high quality, respectful client-centered services and supports for your pet.< /Review>
